<script type="text/javascript">
  try {
    const cookieValue = document.cookie.split(';').find(c => c.trim().startsWith('KP_REF='));
    const referrer = cookieValue ? atob(cookieValue.substring(cookieValue.indexOf('=')+1, cookieValue.length)) : undefined;

    if (referrer !== undefined) {
      Object.defineProperty(document, 'referrer', {
        value: referrer,
        writable: false
      });
    }

    if (cookieValue) {
      document.cookie = 'KP_REF=; Path=/; Expires=Thu, 01 Jan 1970 00:00:00 GMT';
    }
  } catch (err) {}
</script>
